# #dynamic
$scroll_heroes = {
    IF hero_choice < 11: 
        hero_choice += 1
    else
        hero_choice = 1
    END
    gt $curloc
}

$scroll_heroes_back = {
    IF hero_choice > 1: 
        hero_choice -= 1
    else
        hero_choice = 11
    END
    gt $curloc
}

$scroll_ava = {
    IF hero_choice < 12: 
        hero_choice += 1
    else
        hero_choice = 1
    END
    gt $curloc
}

$scroll_ava_back = {
    IF hero_choice > 1: 
        hero_choice -= 1
    else
        hero_choice = 12
    END
    gt $curloc
}

$name_and_start = {
    $estate = 'slum_house'
    $starting_area = 'Slum'
    $a = input ('Give your character a name. Please try to keep this shorter than 14 characters.')
    if $a !'': $master_name = $a
    gt 'start_game'
}

$name_type = {
    $a = input ('Give your character a name. Please try to keep this shorter than 14 characters.')
    if $a !'': $master_name = $a
    gt curloc
}

$go_forward = {
    IF txt < txt_count:
        txt += 1
    else
        delobj '@'
        if $msg_txt ! '' and txt_count = txt:
            msg '<<$msg_txt>>'
            $msg_txt = ''
        END
        GT 'menu_form'
    END
    unsel
    GT curloc
}

$meat_evaluation = {
base_meat_gain = (slave["boobs"] + 2)
if slave["fat"] > 0: base_meat_gain = base_meat_gain*2
mince_gain = 0
mince_bonus = 0
if slave["fat"] = 1: mince_gain = slave["boobs"]
if slave["fat"] = 2: mince_gain = slave["boobs"]*2
if slave["fat"] = 3: mince_gain = slave["boobs"]*3
if slave["fat"] = 4: mince_gain = slave["boobs"]*4
if slave["fat"] = 5: mince_gain = slave["boobs"]*5
if slave["fat"] = 6: mince_gain = slave["boobs"]*5
if slave["fat"] = 7: mince_gain = slave["boobs"]*5
if slave["fat"] = 8: mince_gain = slave["boobs"]*6
if slave["fat"] = 9: mince_gain = slave["boobs"]*6
if slave["fat"] = 10: mince_gain = slave["boobs"]*7
if mince_gain < slave["fat"]: mince_gain = slave["fat"] 
meat_max = 1 + slave["stamina"]
IF base_meat_gain > meat_max:
 meat_gain = meat_max
 mince_bonus = base_meat_gain - meat_max
 else
 meat_gain = base_meat_gain
END
mince_gain += mince_bonus
IF slave['age'] = CONST_INT['loli_age']:
 virgin_meat_gain = meat_gain
 meat_gain = 0
END
!was virginity = 1, error when the butcher gave virgin meat when hymen is restored
IF slave['age'] = CONST_INT['young_age'] and virginity = 0:
 virgin_meat_gain = meat_gain
 meat_gain = 0
END
meat_price = mince_gain + meat_gain*2 + virgin_meat_gain*4
}

$get_meat = {
slave_state = CONST_INT['no_slave'] 
IF frige_space > 0:
 IF frige_space => virgin_meat_gain:
  frige["virgin_meat"] += virgin_meat_gain
  else
  frige["virgin_meat"] += frige_space
 END
END
IF frige_space > 0:
 IF frige_space => meat_gain:
  frige["meat"] += meat_gain
  else
  frige["meat"] += frige_space
 END
END
IF frige_space > 0:
 IF frige_space => mince_gain:
  frige["mince"] += mince_gain
  else
  frige["mince"] += frige_space
 END
END 
}

$get_frige_space = {
    frige_items = frige["vegetables"] + frige["flower"] + frige["spice"] + frige["cheese"] + frige["eggs"] + frige["milk"] + frige["cream"] + frige["mince"] + frige["meat"] + frige["virgin_meat"]
    frige_space = estate_size[$estate] - frige_items
}

$slave_pass_out = {
IF slave_state ! CONST_INT['no_slave']:
 if slave["energy"] = -15: slave_state = CONST_INT['slave_faint']
 IF slave["stamina"] = 0: 
  slave_state = CONST_INT['slave_faint']
  else
  if slave["energy"] > -15: slave_state = CONST_INT['slave_exist']
 END
 IF slave["stamina"] = 0 and slave_rate["stamina"] < 0 and slave['starvation'] > 50: 
  slave_state = CONST_INT['no_slave']
  master_mood['neg_slave_starved'] = 1
  if exam_in_progress ! 1: msg 'Your slave died from starvation. You sold her body to the butcher for 5 sparks.'
  sparks += 5
 END
END

$prisoner_pass_out = {
IF prisoner_state ! 0:
 if prisoner["energy"] = -5: prisoner_state = 2
 IF prisoner["stamina"] = 0: 
  prisoner_state = 2
  else
  if prisoner["energy"] > -5: prisoner_state = 1
 END
 IF prisoner["stamina"] = 0 and prisoner_rate["stamina"] < 0 and prisoner['starvation'] > 50:
  prisoner_state = 0
  msg 'Your prisoner died from starvation, forgotten in dungeon cage. You sold her body to the butcher for 5 sparks.'
  sparks += 5
 END
END
}

$master_pass_out = {
IF master_str <= 0:
 dynamic $death, 'The work so depleted your health that you become seriously ill and had to withdraw from your goal. You will never become a real slave master...'
END
IF master_energy <= -15: gt 'next_day'
}

}

$repulse_check = {
res = slave["obedience"] - repulse + sex_acceptance
if $interaction_type = 'talk': res = slave["obedience"] - repulse
IF $interaction_type = 'master_teaches_slave': res = slave["obedience"] - repulse
IF sex_acceptance < 0: 
 slave_rate["mood"] -= repulse - sex_acceptance
 else
 if erotic_stimulation > 0: res -= slave["arousal"]
END
if slave['domini_dictum'] = 1 and res < 0: res = 0

res_1 = slave_1["obedience"] - repulse_1 + sex_acceptance_1
if $interaction_type = 'talk': res_1 = slave_1["obedience"] - repulse_1
IF $interaction_type = 'master_teaches_sub_slave_1': res_1 = slave_1["obedience"] - repulse_1
IF sex_acceptance_1 < 0: 
 slave_rate_1["mood"] -= repulse_1 - sex_acceptance_1
 else
 if erotic_stimulation_1 > 0: res -= slave_1["arousal"]
END
if slave_1['domini_dictum'] = 1 and res < 0: res_1 = 0

res_2 = slave_2["obedience"] - repulse_2 + sex_acceptance_2
if $interaction_type = 'talk': res_2 = slave_2["obedience"] - repulse_2
IF $interaction_type = 'master_teaches_sub_slave_2': res_2 = slave_2["obedience"] - repulse_2
IF sex_acceptance_2 < 0: 
 slave_rate_2["mood"] -= repulse_2 - sex_acceptance_2
 else
 if erotic_stimulation_2 > 0: res -= slave_2["arousal"]
END
if slave_2['domini_dictum'] = 1 and res < 0: res_2 = 0

res_3 = slave_3["obedience"] - repulse_3 + sex_acceptance_3
if $interaction_type = 'talk': res_3 = slave_3["obedience"] - repulse_3
IF $interaction_type = 'master_teaches_sub_slave_3': res_3 = slave_3["obedience"] - repulse_3
IF sex_acceptance_3 < 0: 
 slave_rate_3["mood"] -= repulse_3 - sex_acceptance_3
 else
 if erotic_stimulation_3 > 0: res -= slave_3["arousal"]
END
if slave_3['domini_dictum'] = 1 and res < 0: res_3 = 0

res_4 = slave_4["obedience"] - repulse_4 + sex_acceptance_4
if $interaction_type = 'talk': res_4 = slave_4["obedience"] - repulse_4
IF $interaction_type = 'master_teaches_sub_slave_4': res_4 = slave_4["obedience"] - repulse_4
IF sex_acceptance_4 < 0: 
 slave_rate_4["mood"] -= repulse_4 - sex_acceptance_4
 else
 if erotic_stimulation_4 > 0: res -= slave_4["arousal"]
END
if slave_4['domini_dictum'] = 1 and res < 0: res_4 = 0

res_5 = slave_5["obedience"] - repulse_5 + sex_acceptance_5
if $interaction_type = 'talk': res_5 = slave_5["obedience"] - repulse_5
IF $interaction_type = 'master_teaches_sub_slave_5': res_5 = slave_5["obedience"] - repulse_5
IF sex_acceptance_5 < 0: 
 slave_rate_5["mood"] -= repulse_5 - sex_acceptance_5
 else
 if erotic_stimulation_5 > 0: res -= slave_5["arousal"]
END
if slave_5['domini_dictum'] = 1 and res < 0: res_5 = 0
}

$sex_acceptance = {
IF shameful > 0:
 sex_acceptance += slave["exhibitionism"] - shameful
 if slave["exhibitionism"] < 1 and slave['neg_shame'] < 1: slave['neg_shame'] = 1
 slave["exhibitionism_xp"] += 1
END
IF painful > 0: 
 sex_acceptance += slave["masohism"] - painful
 if slave["masohism"] < 1 and slave['neg_pain'] < 1: slave['neg_pain'] = 1 
 slave["masohism_xp"] += 1  
END
IF disgusting > 0: 
 sex_acceptance += slave["preversion"] - disgusting
 if slave["preversion"] < 1 and slave['neg_disgust'] < 1: slave['neg_disgust'] = 1  
 slave["preversion_xp"] += 1
END
IF lesbian > 0: 
 sex_acceptance += slave["homosexualism"] - lesbian
 slave["lesbian_xp"] += 1
 else
 if slave["homosexualism"] = 2: sex_acceptance -= 1 
END
IF $interaction_type = 'rape':
 sex_acceptance += slave["arousal"] + slave["sub_vaginal"] + slave["obedience"] - repulse
 if sex_acceptance > 1: sex_acceptance = 1
END
IF shameful_1 > 0:
 sex_acceptance += slave_1["exhibitionism"] - shameful_1
 if slave_1["exhibitionism"] < 1 and slave_1['neg_shame'] < 1: slave_1['neg_shame'] = 1
 slave_1["exhibitionism_xp"] += 1
END

 sex_acceptance += slave_1["masohism"] - painful_1
 if slave_1["masohism"] < 1 and slave_1['neg_pain'] < 1: slave_1['neg_pain'] = 1 
 slave_1["masohism_xp"] += 1  
END

 sex_acceptance += slave_1["preversion"] - disgusting_1

END

$slave_orgasm = {
IF orgasm_prohibited = 0:
 slave_rate["mood"] += final_stimulation
 slave_rate["arousal"] -= final_stimulation
 if slave_rate["arousal"] < 0: slave_rate["arousal"] = 0
 riser = min (master_supermacy, final_stimulation)
 if riser < 0: riser = 1
 slave_rate["instinct"] += riser
 orgasm_description = 1    
 IF slave['pos_orgasm'] < 1: slave['pos_orgasm'] = 1
 slave['neg_horny'] = 0
 else
 IF final_stimulation <= slave["obedience"]:
  slave_rate["arousal"] += final_stimulation
  slave_rate["sensitivity"] += 1
  orgasm_description = 2    
  slave_rate["instinct"] += 1
  slave['neg_horny'] += 1
  else
  slave_rate["mood"] += final_stimulation
  IF slave['pos_orgasm'] < 1: slave['pos_orgasm'] = 1
  slave_rate["arousal"] -= final_stimulation
  if slave_rate["arousal"] < 0: slave_rate["arousal"] = 0
  slave_rate["temper"] += 1
  sin_gained = max (1, slave["moral"])
  if sin_gained > 5: sin_gained = 5
  slave['neg_horny'] = 0
  IF sin_gained => slave["virtue"]:
   slave["virtue"] = 0
   if sin_gained > slave["sin"]: slave["sin"] = sin_gained
   if sententia_veritas = 1: slave["sin"] = 5
  END  
  orgasm_description = 3    
 END
END

 slave_rate_4["instinct"] += riser
 orgasm_description = 1    
 IF slave_4['pos_orgasm'] < 1: slave_4['pos_orgasm'] = 1
 slave_4['neg_horny'] = 0
 else
 IF final_stimulation_4 <= slave_4["obedience"]:
  slave_rate_4["arousal"] += final_stimulation_4
  slave_rate_4["sensitivity"] += 1
  orgasm_description = 2    
  slave_rate_4["instinct"] += 1
  slave_4['neg_horny'] += 1
  else
  slave_rate_4["mood"] += final_stimulation_4
  IF slave_4['pos_orgasm'] < 1: slave_4['pos_orgasm'] = 1
  slave_rate_4["arousal"] -= final_stimulation_4
  if slave_rate_4["arousal"] < 0: slave_rate_4["arousal"] = 0
  slave_rate_4["temper"] += 1
  sin_gained_4 = max (1, slave_4["moral"])
  if sin_gained_4 > 5: sin_gained_4 = 5
  slave_4['neg_horny'] = 0
  IF sin_gained_4 => slave_4["virtue"]:
   slave_4["virtue"] = 0
   if sin_gained_4 > slave_4["sin"]: slave_4["sin"] = sin_gained_4
   if sententia_veritas = 1: slave_4["sin"] = 5
  END  
  orgasm_description = 3    
 END
END

IF orgasm_prohibited_5 = 0:
 slave_rate_5["mood"] += final_stimulation_5
 slave_rate_5["arousal"] -= final_stimulation_5
 if slave_rate_5["arousal"] < 0: slave_rate_5["arousal"] = 0
 riser = min (master_supermacy, final_stimulation_5)
 if riser < 0: riser = 1
 slave_rate_5["instinct"] += riser
 orgasm_description = 1    
 IF slave_5['pos_orgasm'] < 1: slave_5['pos_orgasm'] = 1
 slave_5['neg_horny'] = 0
 else
 IF final_stimulation_5 <= slave_5["obedience"]:
  slave_rate_5["arousal"] += final_stimulation_5
  slave_rate_5["sensitivity"] += 1
  orgasm_description = 2    
  slave_rate_5["instinct"] += 1
  slave_5['neg_horny'] += 1
  else
  slave_rate_5["mood"] += final_stimulation_5
  IF slave_5['pos_orgasm'] < 1: slave_5['pos_orgasm'] = 1
  slave_rate_5["arousal"] -= final_stimulation_5
  if slave_rate_5["arousal"] < 0: slave_rate_5["arousal"] = 0
  slave_rate_5["temper"] += 1
  sin_gained_5 = max (1, slave_5["moral"])
  if sin_gained_5 > 5: sin_gained_5 = 5
  slave_5['neg_horny'] = 0
  IF sin_gained_5 => slave_5["virtue"]:
   slave_5["virtue"] = 0
   if sin_gained_5 > slave_5["sin"]: slave_5["sin"] = sin_gained_5
   if sententia_veritas = 1: slave_5["sin"] = 5
  END  
  orgasm_description = 3    
 END
END
}

 sin_potential = 2 + repulse
 else
 sin_potential = 3
END
if sin_potential > 6: sin_potential = 6
}

$sin_gained_now = {
    IF already_done_today[interaction] = 0:
        sin_gained = sin_potential + res
        if sin_gained <= 0: sin_gained = 1
        if sin_gained > 5: sin_gained = 5
        IF sin_gained => slave["virtue"]:
            slave["virtue"] = 0
            IF sin_gained > slave["sin"]: 
                slave["sin"] = sin_gained
                !TODO: проверить, правильно ли работает исправление
                !Из-за фикса, возможно ухудшение на один день состояния мастера (влияние мудов)
                !master_bad_mood['neg_nice_slave'] = 1
                master_mood['neg_rebell'] = 1
                master_mood['pos_nice_slave'] = 0
                gs '$mod_master_drop', 1
            END 
        END
    END
    if sententia_veritas = 1: slave["virtue"] = 0 & slave["sin"] = 5
}

	IF already_done_today[interaction] = 0:
		virtue_gained = diligence
		if slave_skill > 0: virtue_gained = min (diligence, slave_skill)
		if virtue_gained <= 0: virtue_gained = 1

$complex_diligence = {
complex_diligence = 0
if complex_repulse > slave["obedience"]: complex_diligence = -1
if repulse > slave["obedience"]: complex_diligence = -1
if rebell[$slave_psy_status] > 0: complex_diligence -= 1
if slave['fear'] > complex_repulse: complex_diligence += 1
if slave['mood'] > complex_repulse: complex_diligence += 1
if slave['moral'] > complex_repulse: complex_diligence += 1
if slave['custom'] > complex_repulse: complex_diligence += 1
if slave['rational'] > complex_repulse: complex_diligence += 1
if slave['instinct'] > complex_repulse: complex_diligence += 1
a = slave['spoil'] + complex_repulse
if  a > 10: complex_diligence -= 1
a = slave['pride'] + complex_repulse
if a > 10: complex_diligence -= 1

phobia = 0
IF stimulating > 0: 
 phobia += slave["nymphomania"]
END
IF shameful > 0: phobia += slave["exhibitionism"] - shameful
IF painful > 0: phobia += slave["masohism"] - painful
IF abuse > 0: phobia += slave["abuse_attitude"] - abuse
IF disgusting > 0: phobia += slave["preversion"] - disgusting
IF darkness > 0: phobia += slave["darkness_attitude"] - darkness
IF bloody > 0: phobia += slave["blood_attitude"] - bloody
IF fire_based > 0: phobia += slave["fire_attitude"] - fire_based
IF water_based > 0: phobia += slave["water_attitude"] - water_based
IF vermin_based > 0: phobia += slave["vermin_attitude"] - vermin_based 
IF deprivation > 0: phobia += slave["deprivation_attitude"] - deprivation
complex_diligence += phobia & $dil_message += 'phobia <<phobia>><br>'

if slave['energy'] < 0: complex_diligence += slave['energy']
a = slave['angst'] + complex_repulse
if complex_diligence > 0 and a > 5: complex_diligence -= 1
if slave['moral'] > complex_diligence and slave['moral'] > 0: complex_diligence = slave['moral']
if $slave_psy_status = 'broken': complex_diligence = 0
if complex_diligence > 5: complex_diligence = 5 
if slave['domini_dictum'] = 1 and complex_diligence < 0: complex_diligence = 0
}
$complex_diligence_1 = {
complex_diligence_1 = 0
if complex_repulse_1 > slave_1["obedience"]: complex_diligence_1 = -1
if repulse > slave_1["obedience"]: complex_diligence_1 = -1
if rebell[$slave_psy_status_1] > 0: complex_diligence_1 -= 1

 END

  if $sex['partner'] = '': slave["blood_xp"] += 1
  if $sex['partner'] = 'assistant': assistant["blood_xp"] += 1
 END

 END

 END

 END

 END

 if sex['girl_mood'] > res_3: diligence_3 += 1
 if sex['girl_love'] > res_3: diligence_3 += 1
 if sex['girl_fear'] > res_3: diligence_3 += 1
 if sex['girl_submission'] > res_3: diligence_3 += 1
 if sex['girl_greed'] > res_3: diligence_3 += 1
 if sex['girl_affection'] > res_3: diligence_3 += 1
 if sex['girl_spoil'] + res_3 > 5: diligence_3 -= 1
 if sex['girl_pride'] + res_3 > 5: diligence_3 -= 1
 diligence_3 += phobia_3
 if diligence_3 > 0: if sex['girl_angst'] + res_3 > 5: diligence_3 -= 1
 if sex['girl_love'] > diligence_3: diligence_3 = sex['girl_love']  
 if stimulating > 0 and sex['girl_excitement'] > diligence_3: diligence_3 = sex['girl_excitement']
 if stimulating = 0 and sex['girl_excitement'] > diligence_3: diligence_3 += 1
 if sex['bondage'] = 1: diligence_3 += 1

 if $sex['partner'] = '' and $slave_psy_status = 'broken': diligence_3 = 0
 if sex['girl_energy'] <= 0: diligence_3 = 0
 if diligence_3 > 5: diligence_3 = 5

 IF $sex['partner'] = '' and diligence_3 > 0:
  if repulse > 0:
   slave_rate["custom"] += repulse
   else
   slave_rate["custom"] -= repulse
  end
 END
 
 IF $sex['partner'] = 'assistant' and diligence_3 > 0:
  if repulse > 0:
   assistant_rate["custom"] += repulse
   else
   assistant_rate["custom"] -= repulse
  end
 END
}

$slave_energy_drop = {
slave["energy"] -= 1
if slave["energy"] < -15: slave["energy"] = -15
if slave["energy"] < 0: slave_rate["stamina"] += slave["energy"]
slave["calories"] -= 1
}
$slave_energy_drop_1 = {
slave_1["energy"] -= 1
if slave_1["energy"] < -15: slave_1["energy"] = -15
if slave_1["energy"] < 0: slave_rate_1["stamina"] += slave_1["energy"]
slave_1["calories"] -= 1
}

if slave_2["energy"] < -15: slave_2["energy"] = -15
if slave_2["energy"] < 0: slave_rate_2["stamina"] += slave_2["energy"]
slave_2["calories"] -= 1
}

if assistant["energy"] < -15: assistant["energy"] = -15
if assistant["energy"] < 0: assistant_rate["stamina"] += assistant["energy"]
}

$master_energy_drop = {
master_energy -= 1
if master_energy < -15: master_energy = -15
if master_energy < 0: master_str_rate += master_energy
}

$master_ejaculate = {
IF master_excitement > 0: 
 master_mood_rate += ejaculation_intensity * master_excitement
 if ejaculation_intensity > master_mood['pos_statisfied']: master_mood['pos_statisfied'] = ejaculation_intensity
END
master_excitement -= ejaculation_intensity
IF master_excitement > 0: master_libido += ejaculation_intensity
IF master_excitement < 0: master_libido -= 1
if master_excitement < -5: master_excitement = -5
if master_excitement < 0: dynamic $master_energy_drop
}

$house_cleaning = {
    house_mess_rate = 0
    if house_mess = 1: house_mess_rate = 10
    if house_mess = 2: house_mess_rate = 20
    if house_mess = 3: house_mess_rate = 40
    if house_mess = 4: house_mess_rate = 80
    if house_mess = 5: house_mess_rate = 160
}

$slave_damaged = {
damage += slave["sensitivity"] + slave["hygiene"] - slave["stamina"]
damage += slave_1["sensitivity"] + slave_1["hygiene"] - slave_1["stamina"]
damage += slave_2["sensitivity"] + slave_2["hygiene"] - slave_2["stamina"]
damage += slave_3["sensitivity"] + slave_3["hygiene"] - slave_3["stamina"]
damage += slave_4["sensitivity"] + slave_4["hygiene"] - slave_4["stamina"]
damage += slave_5["sensitivity"] + slave_5["hygiene"] - slave_5["stamina"]
slave_rate["stamina"] -= damage
slave_rate_1["stamina"] -= damage
slave_rate_2["stamina"] -= damage
slave_rate_3["stamina"] -= damage
slave_rate_4["stamina"] -= damage
slave_rate_5["stamina"] -= damage
if damage < 0: damage = 0
if bruising = 1: slave_rate["bruises"] += damage*3
if scarification = 1: slave_rate["scares"] += damage
if bruising = 1: slave_rate_1["bruises"] += damage*3
if scarification = 1: slave_rate_1["scares"] += damage
if bruising = 1: slave_rate_2["bruises"] += damage*3
if scarification = 1: slave_rate_2["scares"] += damage
if bruising = 1: slave_rate_3["bruises"] += damage*3
if scarification = 1: slave_rate_3["scares"] += damage
if bruising = 1: slave_rate_4["bruises"] += damage*3
if scarification = 1: slave_rate_4["scares"] += damage
if bruising = 1: slave_rate_5["bruises"] += damage*3
if scarification = 1: slave_rate_5["scares"] += damage
}

$враг[1] = 'воспитуемая'

slave_1['beaten_ever'] = 1

slave_2['beaten_ever'] = 1

slave_3['beaten_ever'] = 1
slave_4["beaten"] = 1
slave_4['beaten_ever'] = 1
slave_5["beaten"] = 1
slave_5['beaten_ever'] = 1
get_girl = 0
$fight_return = 'menu_form'
copyarr '$display_options', '$edge_of_mists'  
gt 'начать_бой'
}

}



!CHARIOT RACE
$damage_frame = {
IF boards => frame:
 boards -= 1
 else
 frame -= 1
END
}

$damage_wheels = {
IF wheels => chasis:
 wheels -= 1
 else
 chasis -= 1
END
}

$charriot_crush = {
IF charriot['inertion'] > 1:
 frame = 0
 else
 dynamic $damage_frame
END
}

$pony_death = {
charriot['pony_health'] = 0
}

gt 'боевой_интерфейс'
}

GT 'боевой_интерфейс'
}

$оружие = 'безоружный'
gs 'боевое_меню'
GT 'боевой_интерфейс'
}
$убрать_вторичное = {
$вторичный = ''
gs 'боевое_меню'
GT 'боевой_интерфейс'
}

$взять_оружие_за_спиной = {
IF $класс_оружия[$за_спиной]!'вторичное_оружие':
 IF $за_спиной ! 'вторичный':
  $оружие = $за_спиной
  if $класс_оружия[$за_спиной] = 'тяжелое_оружие': $вторичный = ''
  if nogoto = 0: $действия_игрока = 'You pickup the <<$название_предмета[$за_спиной]>>'
  if nogoto = 0: GT 'ход_противников'
 END
END
}
$взять_оружие_слева = {
IF $класс_оружия[$слева]!'вторичное_оружие':
 IF $слева ! $вторичный:
  $оружие = $слева
  if nogoto = 0: $действия_игрока = 'You pickup the <<$название_предмета[$слева]>>'
  if nogoto = 0: GT 'ход_противников'
 END
END
}

$сменить_защиту = {
if $защита[0] = 'контратака': $защита[0] = 'блок' & gt curloc
if $защита[0] = 'уклонение': $защита[0] = 'контратака' & gt curloc
if $защита[0] = 'блок': $защита[0] = 'уклонение' & gt curloc
}

!To show the effects imposed on the Player
$слабость_игрока = {

}

STIFFNESS</font>[<<скованность>>]</a><br>"
}

!Switching between enemies
$переключатель_врагов[1] = {
IF враг[1] = 1:
 $панель_переключений += '[<a href="EXEC:текущий=1&gt''боевой_интерфейс''">1</a>] '
 else
 $панель_переключений += '<font color="silver">[1]</font> '
END
}
$переключатель_врагов[2] = {
IF враг[2] = 1:
 $панель_переключений += '[<a href="EXEC:текущий=2&gt''боевой_интерфейс''">2</a>] '
 else
 $панель_переключений += '<font color="silver">[2]</font> '
END
}
$переключатель_врагов[3] = {
IF враг[3] = 1:
 $панель_переключений += '[<a href="EXEC:текущий=3&gt''боевой_интерфейс''">3</a>] '
 else
 $панель_переключений += '<font color="silver">[3]</font> '
END
}
$переключатель_врагов[4] = {
IF враг[4] = 1:
 $панель_переключений += '[<a href="EXEC:текущий=4&gt''боевой_интерфейс''">4</a>] '
 else
 $панель_переключений += '<font color="silver">[4]</font> '
END
}
$переключатель_врагов[5] = {

 else
 $панель_переключений += '<font color="silver">[5]</font>'
END
}

if кожан > 0: $equip_choice += '<br><a href = "EXEC: $new_item = ''кожан'' & dynamic $slot_1_change">Leather armor [<<кожан>>]</a>'

gt curloc
}

$next_enemy_click = {
текущий += 1
if враг[текущий] ! 1: текущий += 1
if враг[текущий] ! 1: текущий += 1
if враг[текущий] ! 1: текущий += 1
if враг[текущий] ! 1: текущий += 1
gt curloc
}

$prev_enemy_click = {
текущий -= 1
if враг[текущий] ! 1: текущий -= 1
if враг[текущий] ! 1: текущий -= 1
if враг[текущий] ! 1: текущий -= 1
if враг[текущий] ! 1: текущий -= 1
gt curloc
}

$enlarge_breast = {
slave['breast_enchanced'] = 1
slave["boobs"] += 1
if slave["sub_pazuri"] > 0 and slave["sub_pazuri"] < 5: slave["sub_pazuri"] += 1
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_G': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_H' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_G' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EE': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_E': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DD': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EE' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_D': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_E' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CC': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DD' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_C': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_D' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_BB': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CC' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_B': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_C' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_A': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_B' 

if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_FP': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_HP' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EP': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_FP' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DP': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EP' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CP': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DP' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_BP': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CP' 
if $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_AP': $slave["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_BP' 
}

$pierse_clitoris = {
}

$rise_faction_fame = {
no_rise = 0
if $npc_alignment[$npc_id] = 'taurus' and faction_fame['kamira'] > 2: no_rise = 0
if $npc_alignment[$npc_id] = 'serpis' and faction_fame['korvus'] > 2: no_rise = 0
if $npc_alignment[$npc_id] = 'kamira' and faction_fame['taurus'] > 2: no_rise = 0
if $npc_alignment[$npc_id] = 'korvus' and faction_fame['serpis'] > 2: no_rise = 0
if noble_status > 0 and faction_fame[$npc_alignment[$npc_id]] = 5: no_rise = 1
if no_rise = 0: faction_fame[$npc_alignment[$npc_id]] += 1
}

$death = {
    ! Just print the message and wait for click anything for reading verify
    $_d_answer = input($args[0] + ' Restart the game.')
    killvar '$_d_answer'
    gt 'exid'
}

!for controlling starting reputation
$rise_rep = {
IF $estate = 'white_house': msg "This stat is at maximum level."
IF $estate = 'korvus_house':
 IF hero_points => 10:
  hero_points -= 10
  $estate = 'white_house'
  faction_fame['neutral'] = 1
  faction_fame['korvus'] = 0
  $starting_area = 'White Town'
  ELSE
  msg "Not enough character points. You need 10 points to raise this stat."
 END
END
IF $estate = 'taurus_house':
 IF hero_points => 10:
  hero_points -= 10
  $estate = 'korvus_house'
  faction_fame['korvus'] = 1
  faction_fame['taurus'] = 0
  $starting_area = 'Necropolis'
  ELSE
  msg "Not enough character points. You need 10 points to raise this stat."
 END
END
IF $estate = 'serpis_house':
 IF hero_points => 10:
  hero_points -= 10
  $estate = 'taurus_house'
  faction_fame['taurus'] = 1
  faction_fame['serpis'] = 0
  $starting_area = 'Quarter of the Bull'
  ELSE
  msg "Not enough character points. You need 10 points to raise this stat."
 END
END
IF $estate = 'kamira_house':
 IF hero_points => 10:
  hero_points -= 10
  $estate = 'serpis_house'
  faction_fame['serpis'] = 1
  faction_fame['kamira'] = 0
  $starting_area = 'Serpentine Quarter'
  ELSE
  msg "Not enough character points. You need 10 points to raise this stat."
 END
END
IF $estate = 'slum_house':
 IF hero_points => 10:
  hero_points -= 10
  $estate = 'kamira_house'
  faction_fame['kamira'] = 1
  $starting_area = 'Quarter of the Outcasts'
  ELSE
  msg "Not enough character points. You need 10 points to raise this stat."
 END
END
}

$lower_rep = {
IF $estate = 'slum_house': msg "This stat is now at the minimum level."

 hero_points += 10
 $estate = 'slum_house'
 faction_fame['kamira'] = 0
 $starting_area = 'Slum'
END

 hero_points += 10
 $estate = 'kamira_house'
 faction_fame['serpis'] = 0
 faction_fame['kamira'] = 1
 $starting_area = 'Quarter of the Outcasts'

 hero_points += 10

 faction_fame['taurus'] = 0

 $starting_area = 'Serpentine Quarter'

 hero_points += 10
 $estate = 'taurus_house'

 $starting_area = 'Quarter of the Bull'

  hero_points -= 180

  master_bondage = 4
  hero_points -= 40
  else
  msg "Not enough character points. You need 40 points to raise this stat to the fourth level."
 END
END
IF master_bondage = 2:
 IF hero_points => 20:
  master_bondage = 3
  hero_points -= 20
  else
  msg "Not enough character points. You need 20 points to raise this stat to the third level."
 END
END
IF master_bondage = 1:
 IF hero_points => 10:
  master_bondage = 2
  hero_points -= 10
  else
  msg "Not enough character points. You need 10 points to raise this stat to the second level."
 END
END
IF master_bondage = 0:
 IF hero_points => 10:
  master_bondage = 1
  hero_points -= 10
  else
  msg "Not enough character points. You need 10 points to raise this stat to the first level."
 END
END
}

$guro_off = {
no_guro = 1
$bg['slaughter'] = 'empty'
$bg['tabern_kitchen'] = 'empty'
$npc_image['bullhorn'] = ''
}

$guro_on = {
no_guro = 0
$bg['slaughter'] = 'slaughter'
$bg['tabern_kitchen'] = 'tabern_kitchen'
$npc_image['bullhorn'] = 'bullhorn'
}
